『鎌倉サーキット場整備員の手記』
"Notes of Kamakura Circuit Ground Maintenance Staff"

一〇月三一日　第一回大和ＧＰ決勝戦　優勝　タムラ／アベンジ　二位　ヨコタン／スーパーハウンド　三位　アソシエイブル／ＲＧ-一〇ＣＸ
October 31st 1st Yamato GP Final Winner Tamura / Avenge 2nd Place Yokotan / Super Hound 3rd Place Associate / RG-10 CX

※終盤までレースをリードしていたのは翔京ワークスのウルティマ・シュールであったが、一九周目の第一コーナーでクラッシュ。リタイヤした。　尚、騎手は死亡。
* Ultima Sur of Shokyo Works was leading the race until the end of the race, but crashed at the first corner on lap 19. I retired. The jockey died.

※レース終了後の晩、タムラ・アベンジは謎の騎航を行い、クラッシュ。全壊した。　騎手は皇路操であったと思われるが、この日以降、彼女の消息は不明。
* On the evening after the race, Tamura Avenge made a mysterious voyage and crashed. It was completely destroyed. The jockey is believed to have been Ouji Misao, but her whereabouts are unknown after this date.

またほぼ同時刻、タムラのガレージでメカニックの一人が死亡している。　しかしこれについて警察からもタムラからも公的な発表はなく、彼の氏名ほかの素性は明らかでない。
At about the same time, one of the mechanics died in Tamura's garage. However, neither the police nor Tamura have made public announcements about this, and his name and other identities are unknown.

※上記の事件については様々な憶測が飛び交い、一々記す事もできない。また大半は荒唐無稽なものである。　だが、大和ＧＰの背後に装甲競技賭博化を巡る抗争があったことはほぼ事実とみられ、
* Various speculations have been made about the above cases, and it is not possible to write them one by one. Most of them are absurd. However, it seems almost true that there was a conflict over armor competition gambling behind the Yamato GP.

翔京がこれを進め、タムラがこれに反対していた事も、複数の関係者が私的な発言で明らかにしている。
Several officials have also revealed in private statements that Shokyo proceeded with this and Tamura opposed it.

賭博化について愛好者の間では賛否両論だが、大和ＧＰにおける皇路操とアベンジの騎航は既に半ば伝説的であり、あの騎影に想いを寄せ再来を願う風潮は党派の枠を超えて強く――
There are pros and cons among gambling enthusiasts, but the voyage of Ouji Misao and Avenge at the Yamato GP is already half-legendary, and the tendency to think about that gambling shadow and wish for a comeback is strong beyond the boundaries of the faction.

彼らはタムラの姿勢に協調、結集して賭博化反対の宣言を行い、徹底抗戦の構えを見せている。　大和ＧＰで敗れた翔京が賭博化をいまだ断念していないとしても、実現は困難を極めるであろう…………
They cooperated with Tamura's stance, gathered together, declared against gambling, and showed a thorough anti-war stance. Even if Shokyo, who lost in the Yamato GP, has not given up on gambling yet, it will be extremely difficult to realize ...

大鳥香奈枝の後任として横浜の進駐軍総司令部から派遣されて来た新規の八幡宮付将校は、ごく事務的な声で説明を終えると、署長に文書を手渡して退出した。　暫し、沈黙が落ちる。
The new officer with Hachimangu, who was dispatched from Yokohama's General Headquarters to replace Ootori Kanae, handed the document to the chief and left after finishing the explanation with a very clerical voice. For a while, the silence falls.

六波羅の極秘兵器実験。　現今の状況を思えば、それは確かに有り得る話ではあったものの。
Rokuhara's top secret weapon experiment. Given the current situation, it was certainly a possible story.

「………些か、突拍子もない話だとの感慨を禁じ得ません」
“……… I can't help but feel that it's a trivial story.”

「全くだな」
"It's totally"

「あっからさまに胡散臭い話やねぇ……。　幕府の危険な兵器実験。人手不足。現地の警察に協力要請」
"It's an overtly stinky story ... A dangerous weapon test by the Shogunate. Labor shortage. Request cooperation from the local police."

「いっこいっこなら何てこともない話やけど。　三つそろうと……素直に受け止めろって方が無理やわ」

surely. Don't let me feel like I'm reading a play script.

一刀流〝切落〟は敵の一撃に対して全く対称の一撃をもって迎え、これを切り落とし、更に敵の肉体をも断つ技法。　双方が同等の企図をもって打ち合った場合、剣撃の威力と精密さで上回った側が勝利を収める。　今の一合は俺が優越した。　与えた傷は決して浅くない。　これで趨勢が変わった筈！　次の一合で決められるだろう。　　……この男とは、それまでだ。　殺しはしないが動けぬ程に打ち据えて、怪物の相手に向かわねばならない。　そうだ――こんな筋者など。本当は相手取っている場合ではないのだ。　無駄な時間を食わされた……！　返す返すも忌々しい！

それでいながら、尚も昇ってゆく。　あまつさえ、兜角を更に引き上げて。　速力という空の戦いにあっては得難い代価を湯尽し、竜騎兵は高度を貪る。　際限なく。止め処なく。飽き足らず。　天頂へ。　届く筈もなき白の円宮を目掛け。　雪車町は何を思うのか。　追尾を受けてなお方針を翻さないのは、ただ諦めの悪さからか。　当方とて速度はみるみる減殺されている。　だが勢力を充分に確保してのち上昇に転じた村正と、太刀打からそのまま上昇に移った竜騎兵との差は厳然。詰まってはいるものの、優劣は明確に有る。

Without stopping. Not tired. To the zenith. Aiming at the white circle palace that should never reach. What does Sorimachi think? Although it is clogged, there are clear advantages and disadvantages.

打ち間に捕捉するのは時間の問題。　雪車町が迎撃に転じたとしても、態勢を整える前に斬り伏せられる。
It's only a matter of time before you catch it in between. Even if Sorimachi turns to intercept, he will be cut down before he is ready.

What was terrifying was its low-speed control. It's okay to stall normally-no, slowing down to the danger zone where he should be stalling, his invisible reins still control the horse perfectly.

精強さでは人後に落ちない六波羅の正規兵であっても、この域では揚力を手放し、錐揉みして落ちてゆくほかに術を持たないだろう。　百万騎を号す六波羅、その幾人がこの男に倣えるか。　九〇式竜騎兵甲の性能とは到底思われない。　雪車町一蔵の性能に他ならなかった。
Even Rokuhara's regular soldiers, who do not fall behind in terms of strength, will have no choice but to let go of lift and rub them down in this area. 後尾に迫る。　こちらの速力も既に危険域だった。わずかでも気を抜けばその刹那、俺は空から地上へ蹴り落とされるだろう。　間違ってもそんな無様は晒せない。　速度の差はここに至って零に近くなりつつあるも、しかしまだ確在。敵騎はより苛酷な騎航を成し遂げているというに、こちらが先に屈せようか。　あと一歩。　あと一歩で斬れる。
Approaching the tail. This speed was already in the danger zone. If I get rid of it even a little, that moment, I will be kicked from the sky to the ground. 彼我二騎の描く軌道はもはや垂直上昇に近い。　このような騎航は何秒も保たない。　騎体の限度だ。　雪車町が――――

…………That is. Five secret methods inherited from the founder of Ito-ryu, Ito Itosai, from his teacher, Chujo-ryu Kanemaki Jisai.

〝金翅鳥王剣〟
"Golden Bird King Sword"

マックス・インメルマン中尉。　外暦一九一四年から一九一八年にわたって戦われた欧州戦争において、比類なき勇名を鳴り響かせた独逸の誇る撃墜王の一人である。
Lieutenant Max Immelmann. He is one of the proud shooting down kings who made an unparalleled heroic name in the European War, which was fought from 1914 to 1918.

その名に〝侯〟の一語が無い事からも明らかな通り、彼は竜騎兵団に属してはいたものの、騎士階級の出身ではなかった。　真打劔冑の継承者ではなかったのである。
As is clear from the lack of the word "Hou" in his name, he belonged to the Dragoons, but was not from the knighthood. He was not the successor to the true hit tsurugi *.

この時代の撃墜王としては異例と云わねばならない。　外暦一九〇〇年代初頭（国紀二五〇〇年代中盤）はまだ数打劔冑が開発されて間もない頃であり、現在に比べれば性能は著しく低いレベルに留まっていた。
It must be said that it is unusual for a shooting down king of this era. In the early 1900s (mid-2000s), a few hits tsurugi * had just been developed, and its performance remained at a significantly lower level than it is today.

彼が愛騎としたフォッカーＥ３とてもそうだ。　張線支持を採用した単翼騎――当時代の技術の粋が凝らされた騎体ではあったが、真打劔冑との性能差を埋めるものでは到底ない。
The Fokker E3 he loved is so. Single-winged horse that adopted tension wire support-Although it was a horse body with elaborate technology of this era, it can not fill the performance difference of true hit tsurugi * -dono.

その頃、戦場に華を添えた各国の撃墜王――由緒正しい名門の騎士であり最高の劔冑を継承していた人々――と、一介の騎兵将校インメルマンとの間に、騎体性能の点で巨大な隔絶があったことは確実である。
At that time, there was a point of horse performance between the shooting down kings of each country who added glamor to the battlefield-people who were venerable prestigious knights and inherited the best tsurugi * -and one cavalry officer Immelman. It is certain that there was a huge isolation.

しかも、彼の配属された北フランス戦線は敵に正規の騎士が多く、対して味方の騎士は大半が対露戦線に派遣されていたためほとんど皆無という、実に苛酷を極める状況下にあった。
Moreover, the North France front to which he was assigned had many regular knights as enemies, while most of his knights were dispatched to the Russian front, so there were almost no knights, and the situation was extremely harsh.

味方は彼を含めて新弱の竜騎兵ばかり。　敵方は古強の騎士が居並ぶ。　……武功を掲げるどころか、生き残るだけでも至難であったに違いない。
Allies, including him, are all new dragoons. The enemy is lined with old-fashioned knights. It must have been extremely difficult just to survive, rather than to raise martial arts.

その死線にあってインメルマンを撃墜王たらしめたのは、少年期に出会った異国人との体験だった。
At that deadline, it was the experience of a foreigner I met in my childhood that made Immelman the king.

徳川時代の幕引き後、大和はやや閉鎖的であった前時代の反動のように西洋文化を多く取り入れ、何それとなく学んだが、軍事編制においてはプロイセン――ドイツに倣う所が非常に多かった。
After the curtain of the Tokugawa era, Yamato took in a lot of Western culture and learned somehow like the reaction of the previous era, which was a little closed, but in military organization there were many places that imitated Prussia-Germany.

プロイセン軍こそ欧州最精強と見る向きが強かったためである。　幾度となく軍事交流団が派遣され、貪欲に技術知識を求めた。
This is because the Prussian army was strongly regarded as the strongest in Europe. Military exchange teams were dispatched many times and greedily sought technical knowledge.

そうして、ドイツに渡った男の一人に……
Then, to one of the men who went to Germany ...

小野派一刀流一六代宗家、笹木純蔵がいたのだ。
There was Junzo Sasaki, the 16th Soke of the Ono school Ichiroku style.

彼はふとした事から知り合ったインメルマン少年に、一刀流剣術を手解きし、その才の尋常ならざるを知るや、奥義の伝授まで行った。……軽々しいというか、気前が良いというか、いささか変人だったようである。
He learned the Ito-ryu swordsmanship to the Immelman boy he met by accident, and when he learned that his talent was extraordinary, he even taught the mystery. ...... It seems that he was a little weird, light or generous.

だが彼は帰国の後、国粋の文化を売ったとしてこの行為に批判を浴びると、こう応えて一蹴した。　――学ぶのみで教えぬ者は、即ち知恵の盗人である。自分はドイツ軍に学び、返礼として少年に教えたのだ。
However, after returning to Japan, he was criticized for selling the national culture, and he dismissed it in response. --A person who only learns and does not teach is a thief of wisdom. I learned from the German army and taught the boy in return.

かくしてインメルマンは一刀流の秘奥を拝受したのだが、教えた笹木にして彼がその秘技を活用できるだろうとまでは考えていなかったに違いない。
Thus, Immelman received the secret of the one-sword style, but he must not have thought that he could utilize the secret technique with Sasaki who taught him.

一刀流五箇の秘伝は絶えず伝えられてきてこそいたものの、余りの難解さに使い得た者は始祖以来ついになく、技術ではなく単なる知識になり果てていた。　免許皆伝を示す一種の形式に過ぎなかったのである。
Although the secrets of the five Ito-ryu styles have been constantly passed down, no one has been able to use them for too much difficulty since their ancestors, and they have become mere knowledge rather than technology. It was just a kind of form showing all licenses.

だが、北仏戦線の極限状況にあって――　敵の剛強な騎士に追われたマックス・インメルマンは、差し迫る死に抗う渦中で遂に、秘剣の一つを蘇生させるに至ったのだ。
However, in the extreme situation of the Northern French Front-after being chased by a mighty enemy knight, Max Immelmann finally revived one of his secret swords in a whirlpool of imminent death.

金翅鳥王剣。　垂直騎航からの反転落下攻撃。　自己より圧倒的に優る敵を討つ、起死回生の剣。
Golden Bird King Sword. Reverse fall attack from vertical cavalry. A sword of rebirth that defeats enemies that are overwhelmingly superior to oneself.

以後、インメルマンは常にこの技と共にあり、幾多の騎士を空から墜として敵味方を瞠目させた。　彼と彼の技は同一視され、その名は欧州を席巻し、悪魔的な恐怖と戦神的な畏怖の的となった。
Since then, Immelman has always been with this technique, dropping many knights from the sky and staring at his enemies and allies. He and his skill were equated, and the name swept Europe and became the target of demonic horror and war-god awe.

一九一六年に戦死するまで、生涯の撃墜数は一七騎。　全てがフランスの名だたる騎士である。
Until he died in 1916, he shot down 17 horses in his lifetime. All are famous knights of France.

現在なおその名は語り継がれ、知らぬ者とていない。　最強、無敵、魔剣、神技――彼の死と共に消え失せた、戦場の幻影を示すものとして、諸国の軍人そして歴史書はその名をいつまでも叫び続ける。
Even now, the name has been handed down, and he is not a stranger. The strongest, invincible, magic sword, divine technique-military personnel and history books of the nations continue to scream their name as an indication of the illusion of the battlefield that disappeared with his death.

〝インメルマンの反転〟と。
With "Reversal of Immelman".

《みど……っ……いる?　きっ……ぃを………ない………》

Muramasa's voice is far away. The field of vision is dull-vermilion. How much damage did you get? The consciousness of working like other people's affairs was inferred from the current situation. dying. It's strange to be alive. No, it may be dying. ...... Golden winged bird king sword. I never thought that such a ghost would crawl out of the graveyard. It is said that there is no successor to Immelman. His sword ended up being his own technique. Horse body control ability to survive the stall. It's more natural than a grudge that no one after him had such a thing. Even though. This man--

Dazzling. Am I still sailing? Is it still within a momentary time ... Or is it just that I haven't realized that it's actually falling ... Neither is clear.

《み……っ…！　か…避……っ！》

世界が激しく揺れ動く。　それもまた、己の事として感じられない。　痛みがないからだろう。　深々と、肉体の何処かが切り裂かれている筈なのに、神経からの信号がない。　もう、麻痺してしまっているのか。　信号を受け取るべき脳が破損したか……

There is an individual who challenges a huge power person. That fact surely harbors the light of courage in people's hearts. Eventually, it grows into the power to crush oppression.

筆は剣よりも強いのだ、そう彼は主張した。　それが彼の信念だった。
The brush is mightier than the sword, he insisted. That was his belief.

あなたを報道させてくれと、彼は俺に懇願した。　自分のやり方で、あなたと一緒に戦いたい。そうも言った。
He begged me to report you. I want to fight with you in my own way. I also said so.

俺の同意を得られないと知ると、彼は自分の覚悟を見せようと思ったのか、俺を襲った殺人鬼――青江だ――について調べ上げ、遂に所在を突き止めるという真似までやって見せた。
When he found out that he couldn't get my consent, he might have decided to show his resolve, and he investigated the murderer who attacked me-Aoe-and finally found out where he was. It was.

代償は腕一本を失う重傷であった。　青江を仕留め、病室を見舞った俺に、彼は微笑んで言った。ペンが剣を一本折った、自分の信念の勝利だ、と。
The price was a serious injury, losing one arm. He smiled and said to me, who had killed Aoe and visited the hospital room. Pen broke a sword, a victory for his belief.

彼は正しかった。俺が殺人鬼を倒せたのは彼の助力のお陰だった。　そう告げると、彼は照れ臭そうに目を伏せた。
He was right. It was thanks to his help that I was able to defeat the murderer. When he said so, he looked down with a shy look.

その首を刎ねた。　　　ペンは折れた。
I decapitated the neck. The pen broke.

俺は彼の信念を侮辱した。
I insulted his belief.

……それは後に元寇と呼ばれる事変であることを、一条は知っている。
... Ichijou knows that it is an incident later called the Mongol invasion.

彼ははじめ、相模國に住む一介の村鍛冶であった。　鋤、鍬といった農具から馬蹄、又は包丁など、村の穏やかな生活の中で求められる全てを拵えた。
At first, he was a village smith who lived in Sagami Province. From farm tools such as plows and hoe to horseshoes or kitchen knives, everything required in the peaceful life of the village was taken.

勿論、劒冑などは造らない。　村の生活には無用であるし、そもそも一介の村鍛冶がそんな業を心得ていよう筈もない。
Of course, we don't make tsurugi. It is useless for the life of the village, and there is no way that a village blacksmith would know such a work in the first place.

だが刀剣は、少々打った。　時折山から下りてくる野犬の類や、幕府の膝元たる関東では滅多に見ないが皆無でもない流賊などから、村を守るために求められたのだ。
But the sword struck a little. They were asked to protect the village from the stray dogs that occasionally descended from the mountains and the bandits that are rarely seen in the Kanto region, which is the foot of the shogunate.

そんな中の一振りがある時、村を治める領主の目に留まった。　粗末だが、名もなき村鍛冶にはふさわしからぬ出来――と、領主は些かの感興を持って彼の事を記憶した。
When there was a swing, it caught the eye of the lord who governed the village. Poor, but unsuitable for a nameless village smith-the lord remembered him with a little excitement.

そのせいだろう。　弘安四年、幕府はかつてない大動員令を発し、主将として執権の弟を派遣する。領主はその直属軍に一族郎党を連れ参じたが、その際、彼に陣中鍛冶を命じた。
Probably because of that. In the 4th year of Koan, the Shogunate issued an unprecedented mobilization order and dispatched a younger brother in power as captain. The lord brought the Clan Roh Party to his direct army, at which time he ordered him to smith.

その戦のことを、彼は何も知らなかった。　雑用役の下人に交じって働きながら、己が錆を落とした古刀で何物を斬るのか、破損を繕ってやった鎧で何から身を守るのか、何も知らず日々を過ごした。
He knew nothing about the battle. While working with a servant of a chore, I spent my days knowing nothing about what I would cut with a rusted old sword and what I would protect myself from with armor that had been repaired for damage.

どうでも良いことだった。　大方またどこぞの豪族が鎌倉様に反旗を翻し、それを討伐にゆくのだろうが、そんなもの、彼にも村にも何の関わりもない。
It didn't matter. Most of the great tribes will rebel against Kamakura and go to subdue it, but that has nothing to do with him or the village.

戦が長引けば自分が陣中に留められる期間も長引くし、村からの徴発も厳しくなるだろう。　だから早く終わって欲しい。そう願うだけだった。
The longer the battle, the longer you will stay in the camp, and the more severe the charges from the village will be. So I want you to finish early. I just hoped so.

行軍の日々は長く続いた。　やがて海に面し、船を仕立てて更にその向こうの陸まで渡る段になって、彼はようやく自分が大和の果て――九州を目指していることに気付いた。
The days of the march lasted a long time. Eventually, facing the sea, he set up a ship and crossed over to the land beyond, and he finally realized that he was heading for the end of Yamato-Kyushu.

一体どうして、そんな所へ関東の兵を送らねばならないのか。近辺に所領を持つ御家人らだけで充分ではないか？　彼は下人衆と揃って首を傾げたが、答は出なかった。
Why should we send Kanto soldiers to such a place? Isn't it enough for the gokenins who have territories in the vicinity? He tilted his head with the crowd, but no answer was given.

勿論、下人風情にいちいち説明をしてくれる気安い武士などいない。　彼らが真相を朧に察し得たのは、再び海岸に達し、そこで海に向かって布陣する大軍勢を見た時だった。
Of course, there is no easy-going samurai who can explain to the servants. It was only when they reached the shore again that they saw a large army arranging towards the sea.

――敵は、海を渡って来るのだ。　御伽噺に聞くばかりの、唐天竺からやって来るのだ。
-The enemy is crossing the sea. It comes from Kara Tenjiku, which you just listen to in the storyteller.

陣では現地の庶民が多数働いていて、彼らから話を聞くことができた。〝敵〟は既に幾つかの島々を襲い、甚大な被害をもたらしているという。
Many local people were working in the camp, and I was able to hear from them. It is said that the "enemy" has already attacked several islands and caused enormous damage.

この博多も敵の先遣隊であろう武者団の襲撃を数度に渡って受けており、その都度、迎撃に出た大和武者が少なからず討ち死にしているという。　頼朝公以来常勝を以て鳴る御家人衆が、だ。
This Hakata has also been attacked by the musha corps, which is supposed to be the enemy's advance corps, several times, and it is said that Yamato musha who went out to intercept each time was killed not a little. The Gokenin who have been ringing with a constant victory since Yoritomo.

敵の武者はとにかく小回りが利き、御家人衆は速度では優りながら運動に付いてゆくことができず、上を押さえられて次々と墜とされてしまう……。　飯番の老人は恐ろしげに、そう語った。
The enemy musha has a small turn, and the Gokenin cannot keep up with the movement while being superior in speed, and they are held down and crashed one after another. The old man in the rice cooked horribly said so.

そんな奴らに、自分の打つ刀などがどれほどの役に立とう？　彼は初めて不安に駆られた。
How useful are your swords to those guys? He was anxious for the first time.

それは彼を連れてきた領主も同じであったらしい。　わざわざ彼を呼びつけて、決して仕事に手を抜いてはならぬ、取り立ててやった恩を仇で返すでないぞと、苛立たしげに一喝した。
It seems that the lord who brought him was the same. He called him all the way, and frustratedly said that he should never cut corners in his work and that he would not give back the favor he had collected.

彼は恐懼して承った。　が、実際にやったのは、下人仲間に倣っていつでも逃げられるよう身の回りの物をまとめておく事だった。
He was terrified and accepted. However, what I actually did was to imitate my fellow servants and keep things around me so that I could escape at any time.

迷惑ならともかく恩など受けた覚えはなかったし、仮にあったとしても命を捨てて報いるなど御免だった。　海の向こうの異国を相手取る戦であっても、彼に何の関わりもないという意味では全く同じだ。
I didn't remember receiving any gratitude if it was a nuisance, and even if it was, I was sorry to give up my life and reward it. It's exactly the same in the sense that it has nothing to do with him, even in a battle against a foreign country over the sea.

命を拾うことだけが大事、村に帰ることだけが大事だった。　戦など、やりたい連中だけでやっていれば良いのだ。
It was only important to get a life, and only to return to the village. You only have to do it with the people you want to do, such as battles.

この戦でもし御家人衆が負けたとしても、まさか敵が関東まで攻め上ってくることはなかろうし。　九州一帯は大変なことになるかもしれないが……同情以上の何かをする責任など自分には無い。
Even if the Gokenins lose in this battle, the enemy will not attack Kanto. The whole area of ​​Kyushu may be difficult, but ... I have no responsibility to do anything more than sympathy.

彼はそう思っていた。　それに、異国の兵といえど所詮は同じ人間。
He thought so. Besides, even though they are foreign soldiers, they are the same human beings.

周囲では敵の蒙古なる奴輩は人ならぬ悪鬼の群れで、血を杯に満たして呑み人肉に舌鼓を打つ、などの噂がまことしやかに囁かれていたが――この点、彼の認識は醒めたものだった。
Rumors were whispered around him that the enemy, Mongolian, was a group of demons who weren't humans, filled with blood, swallowed, and sipped on human flesh. The recognition of was awakened.

不純を廃して純なるものに鍛え上げる鍛冶を生業とするためであろうか。彼は単純に、敵軍にもこちらと同じように船や劒冑があるらしい、ならそれを使うのも我々と同じような人間だろう――と考えていた。
Is it because the blacksmith who abolishes the impure and trains it into a pure one is his business? He simply thought that the enemy army would have ships and tsurugi as well, and that they would be the same people as us.

つまりは万が一、大和の全てが征服されてしまったとしても、それは支配者が幕府から別の誰かに変わるだけの話。　やっぱりどうでも良い事だと、彼は結論した。
In other words, even if all of Yamato were conquered, it would just change the ruler from the shogunate to someone else. He concluded that it didn't matter.

そうして迎えた、決戦の日。　水平線を黒い影が埋め尽くした。
Then, the day of the decisive battle. The horizon was filled with black shadows.

押し寄せてくる船、船、船。　その上空を旋回する幾多の武者。
Ships, ships, ships rushing in. Many mushas orbiting over it.

博多に陣取る、西国の兵の総結集と言って良かろう大軍の、更に倍ほどもいようか。　下人仲間の幾人かは早くも逃げ出し、武士らはそれを咎めるのも忘れて戦慄した。
Is it about twice as much as the large army that can be said to be a rally of Western soldiers in Hakata? Some of his fellow servants ran away as soon as possible, and the samurai were terrified, forgetting to blame them.

その中で、彼が仲間と共に逃げなかったのは、無論、勇気を振り絞ったからではない。　戦闘が始まってから混乱に紛れて逃げ出した方が、後々無難であろうと小賢しく計算しただけの事だ。
Of course, he didn't run away with his companions because of his courage. It's just a wise calculation that it would be safer to escape in the turmoil after the battle began.

――しかし。　その卑しい小知が、彼という人間の運命を決した。
--However. That lowly wisdom determined the fate of a human being, he.

威嚇のつもりか、金物を打ち鳴らしつつ、蒙古なる敵軍は博多へ迫る。　大和軍は陣を固め、息を呑んで待ち受け……
The enemy army of Mongolia approaches Hakata while beating the hardware, perhaps as a threat. The Yamato Army solidifies its camp, holds its breath and waits ...

やがて。　それまでとは全く別種の慄きに、血の気を失った。
Eventually. I lost my blood in a completely different kind of horror.

最初に気付いたのは弓衆の幾人か――特に眼の良い人々だった。　突如絶句し、あるいは掠れた呻き声を上げる彼らに、周囲は訝り。しかし程なく、その理由を知った。
The first things I noticed were some of the archers-especially those with good eyesight. The people around me wondered at them who suddenly screamed or moaned. But soon I found out why.

誰もが見た。彼も見た。　船の上で繰り広げられている光景を。
Everyone saw it. He also saw. The sight unfolding on the ship.

女が並んでいた。　大和人の女だった。
The women were lined up. It was a Yamato woman.

皆一様に、四足獣よろしく尻を突き出していた。　全裸だった。
Everyone was uniformly sticking out their hips like a four-legged beast. I was naked.

差し出した尻は、異装の男たちに抱え込まれている。　顔形、風体、仲間と交わす野卑な言語、甲高い笑い。どれをとっても大和人ではない。
The ass that I presented is held by men in disguise. Face shape, style, savage language with friends, high-pitched laughter. None of them are Yamato people.

異人が、大和の女を姦している。　泣き叫ぶ声に、哄笑を返しながら。
A stranger is raping a Yamato woman. While laughing back at the crying voice.

……蒙古に襲われた島では、男は一人残らず殺され、女は攫われたそうな……。　敵にまつわる無数の噂の中にはそんなものもあったと、彼は思い出していた。
On the island attacked by Mongolia, all the men were killed and the women were kidnapped. He remembered that some of the myriad rumors about the enemy were.

女たちは逃げもせず、暴行を受け止めている。　船の中では逃げようとてあるまいが。しかし、それだけではなかった。
The women do not run away and accept the assault. I'm not trying to escape on the ship. But that wasn't the only thing.

彼女らは船に繋がれている。　手の甲に穴を開けられ、そこに通された鎖で繋がれている。
They are connected to a ship. A hole is made in the back of the hand, and it is connected by a chain passed through it.

それでは逃げられる筈がなかった。　つまりは家畜と同じ扱いを受けているのだから。
Then I couldn't escape. In other words, they are treated the same as livestock.

女は皆、若い。　花の盛りか、開き頃か、蕾の頃。
All the women are young. When the flowers are in full bloom, when they open, or when they are buds.

小さな娘が何人もの兵に代わる代わる犯されていた。　兵らは、未熟な性器へ無理矢理に突き込む行為だけを楽しんでいるらしい。
A little daughter was being raped in place of several soldiers. The soldiers seem to enjoy only the act of forcing them into their immature genitals.

最後は巨躯の兵士だった。　彼はどうしても入れる事ができなかったようだ。
The last was a giant soldier. He just couldn't get in.

周囲の仲間が下品な嘲笑を浴びせる。　兵士は頬を紅潮させると、その腹いせだろう、悶絶する娘の顔面を容赦なく殴りつけ、潰し、船の縁から放り捨てた。
The people around me make a vulgar ridicule. When the soldier flushed his cheeks, he mercilessly beat, crushed, and threw him off the edge of the ship, his angry, fainting daughter's face.

鎖で、娘の亡骸が吊り下げられる。　見れば、そんな飾りはどの船にもあった。
A chain hangs the body of her daughter. If you look, there was such a decoration on every ship.

ある船では、大槍で串刺しにされた女が舷側にぶら下がっていた。
On one ship, a woman skewered with a large spear was hanging on the side.

ある船では、女が分解され、それぞれ別個に吊るされていた。
On one ship, the woman was disassembled and hung separately.

ある船では、まだ生きている女が幾人も。　……その船の飾りは、他と比べても際立った特徴を持つようであった。
On one ship, there are many women who are still alive. ...... The decoration of the ship seemed to have a distinctive feature compared to others.

女達は、比較的年嵩。　そして必ず、小さな物体を首に括りつけられている。
Women are relatively old. And there is always a small object tied around his neck.

物体。そう、物体だ。　　物体としか呼びようはない。生命を持たないものは。かつては持っていたのだとしても。
object. Yes, it's an object. It can only be called an object. Those who do not have life. Even if I used to have it.

女の発する、音程の狂った慟哭の叫びを聴きながら、船の上で兵士達が笑う。　手を打ち、さも楽しげに。
Soldiers laugh on the ship as they listen to the screams of the crazy roar of the woman. Clap your hands and have fun.

――――そんな光景が、
―――― Such a scene

それは最早、人間の所業ではなかった。　断じて違った。
It was no longer the work of humans. It was definitely different.

こんな事をする者は、もう人間ではない。
Those who do this are no longer humans.

彼は知った。　世界の真実を一つ知った。
He knew. I knew one truth of the world.

そう悟ったのは彼だけではなかったろう。　下人仲間も皆、同じ思いを抱いた筈だ。
He wasn't the only one who realized that. All my fellow servants should have the same feelings.

しかし仲間たちは、絶望にへたり込むか、あるいは狂ったように喚きつつ逃げ出すか、どちらかを選んだ。　彼だけが違った。
But their companions chose to either fall into despair or scream like crazy and run away. Only he was different.

彼は絶望しなかった。
He didn't despair.

敵の武者が空襲を開始する。　その支援下、兵士達が小船に乗り移り、浜辺へ殺到する。
Enemy musha launches an air raid. With that support, soldiers transfer to a small boat and rush to the beach.

彼はその前へ躍り出た。　誰よりも早く。
He jumped before that. Faster than anyone.

ろくに喧嘩をした事もない拳に自前の刀を握り締め、　鎧もなく、薄衣一枚きりの姿で。
He clasped his own sword to his fist, which he had never quarreled with, without armor, and in a thin coat.

無数の毒矢が、恐ろしい音とともに爆裂する怪球が飛び交う戦場の直中を駆け抜ける。
Countless poison darts run through the battlefield where monster balls explode with a terrifying sound.

何も考えてはいなかった。　考えるという事は、必要なかった。
I wasn't thinking about anything. I didn't need to think.

その時の――それからの彼は、ただ一つの意思の塊だった。
At that time-then he was the only mass of will.

彼はただの『彼』として歴史に埋もれる運命を捨て、　大和史上に不朽不滅の名を残す道を辿る事になった。
He abandoned his destiny as a mere "he" and decided to follow the path of leaving an immortal name in the history of Yamato.

……彼は生き延びた。　剣の心得もない彼が重傷を負いながらも命を拾ったのは、まず奇跡的というべきだろう。
... he survived. It must be miraculous that he, who had no knowledge of the sword, was seriously injured but died.

下人輩に先を行かせてなるものかと奮起して彼の前へ飛び出した者や、また身分に相応しからぬ彼の行動に感銘を受けて守ってやろうとした者が、武士の中に幾人かいたためであるかもしれない。
Among the samurai, there are those who jumped out in front of him, wondering if he would let his juniors go ahead, and those who were impressed by his behavior that was not suitable for his status and tried to protect him. It may be because there were several people in the area.

戦も、大和の勝利であった。　敵勢の猛攻には苦しめられたものの、よく抗戦してこれを支え――そして訪れた台風が、最終的に海上の軍勢を一息で吹き散らしたからだ。
The battle was also Yamato's victory. Despite suffering from the onslaught of the enemy, he often fought to support it-and the typhoon that came finally blew away the maritime forces.

神仏の加護、天罰覿面と、人々は沸き返った。　彼はそれを否定こそしなかったものの、喜びに同調はしなかった。
People were boiled with the blessing of the gods and Buddha and the punishment. He didn't deny it, but he didn't go along with joy.

神仏は遅過ぎる。　神風とやらが吹いたのは、戦いの趨勢がほぼ決し、蒙古軍が橋頭堡を捨て船へ撤退した後だった。
God and Buddha are too late. The kamikaze blew after the battle trend was almost decided and the Mongolian army abandoned the bridgehead and withdrew to the ship.

そんな頼りない力をあてにしてはいられない。　彼はもう、知っているのだ。この世には悪があるという事を。
I can't count on such unreliable power. He already knows. That there is evil in this world.

それは決して、蒙古軍だけに留まらない事も。　蒙古も人であった。ならば悪鬼は人から生まれる。人在る限り、いつでもどこにでも悪鬼は生じ得るのだ。
It is by no means limited to the Mongolian army. Mongolia was also a person. Then the devil is born from a person. As long as there are people, demons can occur anytime, anywhere.

彼は戦場を駆けた勢いそのままに、一人、傷もまだ癒えぬ身体を抱えて関東へ戻った。　だが、故郷へは足も向けなかった。
With the momentum of running on the battlefield, he returned to Kanto with a body that could not heal his wounds. However, he didn't even go to his hometown.

彼は鎌倉へ入り、新藤五国光の門を叩いた。　当時、関東随一と名高かった劒冑鍛冶である。
He entered Kamakura and hit the gate of Shinto Gokunimitsu. At that time, it was the best tsurugi smith in the Kanto region.

――悪を討つは人の力。　人の力の極峰たる劒冑こそ、求めねばならぬ。
--It is human power to avenge evil. Tsurugi, the ultimate in human power, must be sought.

そう確信して、彼は入門を懇請した。　これは、論外の所業である。
Convinced so, he begged for an introduction. This is an out-of-the-box work.

劒冑を鍛え上げる業は父祖代々、親から子へ伝えてゆくもの。　縁も所縁も無い他人に教えるようなものではない。
The work of training tsurugi is passed down from parents to children from generation to generation. It's not like teaching someone who has no ties or ties.

しかも、業の伝授はごく幼少の頃から行われる。　彼のように成年を過ぎてから修行を開始するなど、およそ前例がない。
Moreover, the teaching of karma is carried out from a very young age. It is almost unprecedented to start training after adulthood like him.

更に、彼は普通の大和人である。　生来の鍛冶師たる蝦夷ではなく。もし業成って劒冑を造り得ても、その出来は決して蝦夷の作に及ばぬであろう。
Moreover, he is an ordinary Yamato. Not Ezo, a natural blacksmith. Even if it were possible to make tsurugi by doing business, the result would never be as good as Ezo's work.

当代国光、そしてその親族にして弟子である人々の誰もが訴えを一笑に付し、また世に悪鬼在り、これを討つべしと繰り返す男を狂人と見て恐ろしくも思い、門前払いにしようとした。
Kunimitsu of the present generation, and all of his relatives and disciples, laughed at the complaint, and saw a man who was a demon in the world and repeated this as a madman, and tried to pay in advance.

それを止めたのは、当代国光の叔父にあたる人物である。
The person who stopped it was the uncle of Kunimitsu.

……鍛冶一門の技術継承は、基本的に親と子の間で行われる。　親は子に技術の全てを伝えた後、己の肉体を劒冑に変える。子はそれを見届ける。
…… The technology inheritance of the blacksmith family is basically carried out between parents and children. After telling the child all the techniques, the parent turns his body into tsurugi. The child sees it.

しかしこの形態は、万一伝授に失陥があった場合、取り返しのつかなくなる危険を孕んでいる。　改めて教えを乞おうにも、先代は既に冷たい甲鉄であるからだ。
However, this form carries the risk of being irreparable in the unlikely event of a failure in teaching. Even if I ask for the teaching again, the predecessor is already a cold iron.

そのような事態に備え、鍛冶師の子息のうち末弟にあたる者は、劒冑に成らず、一門の教育補佐役として生涯を終えるよう求められるのが通例である。　当代国光の叔父が、つまりそれであった。
In preparation for such a situation, the youngest of the blacksmith's sons is usually required to end his life as a family of educational assistants instead of becoming tsurugi. That was Kunimitsu's uncle.

泡を吹いて喚き散らす男をじっと観察していた叔父は、いよいよ一同が彼を放り出そうとする段になるやそれを制し、奥へと通した。　そして、告げた。
The uncle, who was watching the man blowing bubbles and screaming, finally controlled it when it was time for everyone to throw him out, and let him go deeper. And I told him.

――おのれはまさしく天命の劒冑鍛冶である。　これまで幾人もの親族を育て上げ、劒冑として送り出してきたが、おのれをそうするのに彼らの誰よりも短い年月しか必要とはせぬであろう――
-I'm just a mortal tsurugi smith. I've raised a number of relatives and sent them out as tsurugi, but it will only take less than any of them to do that--

国光の叔父は慧眼であった。　劒冑鍛錬とは、己の身魂を異なるモノへと変貌せしめる鍛冶の事。
Kunimitsu's uncle was an eye-opener. Tsurugi smithing is a smithing that transforms your soul into something different.

既に自分の魂の形を知り、目指すべき形をも知る彼は、鍛冶師修行における最も困難な過程をはや終えていたに等しく、後は専門の技術しか必要ではなかった。　……その日より、僅か数年。
Already knowing the shape of his soul and knowing what he should aim for, he had almost completed the most difficult process of blacksmith training, and only required specialized skills. …… Only a few years from that day.

相州五郎入道〝正宗〟。　彼の理想は、かく実現した。
Sagami Goro entrance "Masamune". His ideal has come true.

破邪の劒冑。　蝦夷の手によらぬ、しかし天下無双の大名甲。
Tsurugi of brutality. It's not in the hands of Ezo, but it's a daimyo in the world.

誰もが、その劒冑の美しさを認めた。　誰もが、その美が意味する甲鉄の堅牢さを悟った。
Everyone acknowledged the beauty of that tsurugi. Everyone realized the robustness of the ironclad that its beauty meant.

大和人の鍛冶師が、これほどの作甲を成し得るとは。　蝦夷鍛冶は自信を打ち砕かれて絶句し、長年蝦夷の風下に立たされてきた大和鍛冶は大きな希望を抱いた。
It is possible that a Yamato blacksmith can make such an armor. Ezo Blacksmith shattered his confidence and broke down, and Yamato Blacksmith, who had been standing on the leeward side of Ezo for many years, had great hope.

彼が仕手を得て、望み通りの活躍を果たしたならば、彼の名と姿形は更に知れ渡り、多くの大和鍛冶が彼に続き――遂には蝦夷と大和人の鍛冶技術の優劣を覆しさえしたかもしれない。
If he got the job and did what he wanted, his name and appearance would become even more known, and many Yamato blacksmiths would follow him-finally overturning the superiority and inferiority of Ezo and Yamato's blacksmithing techniques. I might even have done it.

そうならなかったのは、皮肉にも、彼正宗が余りに傑出した出来であった為だった。
It didn't happen because, ironically, Masamune was so outstanding.

正宗は打ち上げられて間もなく時の将軍に献上され、やがて帝の上覧に与り、それから後も最高権力者の間を行き来した。　だが、一度たりと装甲される事はなかった。
Shortly after being launched, Masamune was presented to the shogun of the time, eventually attended the Emperor's inspection, and then went back and forth between the highest powers. However, it was never armored.

不可侵性すら感じさせる佇まいを見た歴代の所有者達は、感嘆すると共に畏れを抱き、実用の武具とするよりも神宝として秘めおくことを選んだのである。
Successive owners, who saw the appearance of even inviolability, admired and feared, and chose to keep it as a sacred treasure rather than as a practical armor.

悪を討つべくして劒冑となった彼には、全く心外の成り行きであった。　彼は宝物庫の奥へ秘蔵されつつも伝説の名甲として後世に名を遺したが、そんなことには何の意味もない。
It was a completely unexpected outcome for him, who became tsurugi to avenge evil. Although he is treasured in the back of the treasure house, he left his name as a legendary instep to posterity, but that does not mean anything.

彼は自分と志を同じくする仕手に出会い、戦いの旅に出なくてはならなかったのである。　その望みは果たされることなく、時ばかりが過ぎた。
He had to meet a like-minded man and embark on a battle journey. The hope has not been fulfilled, and time has passed.

五郎正宗は戦国時代に至って織田信長の手に渡った後、本能寺の変を境に表舞台から消え、その後は密かに人手から人手へと渡り、最後はとある山村で厄災を鎮めるための祭具とされて眠りにつく。

Ichijou knows. I know that the incident that Masamune encountered was a war called the Mongol invasion.

喜ぶに喜べないというのが、多くの市民の心情ではなかろうか。　　尤も、俺の内心はまた少し風向きが違う。

「それで、な。　こっちも、ひとつ思い切った手を打とうか……そう考えてるんよ」

"..."

"If you compare the battle over Yamato to shogi, it's a dangerous move that could turn the board over. To be honest, I can't help but ... the situation is imminent. Probably."

「……我々が期待するほどの時間は与えられないだろう。にも拘わらずただ座視するなら、それは大和の未来を擲つことを意味する……。　いや、切り開かねばならん。生存の道は」

呟きの音量で、呼ぶ。　それは先を促す為だったのか、制止の為だったのか、自分でも判じかねた。
Call with the volume of muttering. I couldn't tell whether it was to encourage the future or to stop it.

なにやら迂回している署長の言葉が、最終的に何処へ行き着くのか、悟らずに済むほど俺も鈍感ではいられなかった。
I couldn't be so insensitive that I didn't have to realize where the detoured chief's words would end up.

「敵の勢力は強大を極める。　対するに、我々は弱小そのものだ」
"The power of the enemy is extremely powerful. On the other hand, we are weak and weak."

弱小勢力の常套手段。　警察職にある人間として決して認められぬであろうその行為を、しかし署長は黙示した。
A common practice for weak powers. The chief, however, implied the act, which would never be recognized as a human being in the police position.

「……そこまで追い詰められていると……」
"... If you're cornered to that point ..."

「本当に追い詰められるまでもう時間がない、という意味だがな」

死刑判決を下されてしまえばそれで最後。執行まで何年あろうともはや死の運命は覆せない、という事か。　……否定はできなかった。
If you are sentenced to death, that's the end. Does that mean that the fate of death can no longer be overturned no matter how many years it takes to execute it? ... I couldn't deny it.

「標的は……」

「……」

"It cannot be an expeditionary force. Even if the leaders of the expeditionary force are successfully destroyed, a substitute officers will be dispatched from the UN headquarters."

親王も署長も、何も言ってはこない。　しかし、その沈黙――否定しないという事実こそが返答であろう。

"It was natural for other countries to do so. In the past, there were precedents for the Fujiwara and Taira administrations, and everyone would have hoped to inherit that form ..."

「だが藤原氏や平氏が朝廷権力と密着したのに対して、源氏は朝廷から距離を取った。　朝廷は京都に据え置いたまま、東の鎌倉に新たな都を造った。政権と朝廷を分離した」
"But while Mr. Fujiwara and Mr. Taira were in close contact with the imperial court power, Genji moved away from the imperial court. The imperial court remained in Kyoto and built a new city in eastern Kamakura. separated"

「自らの政権を朝廷に承認させる形式をとる事で、朝廷の権威を保障しつつそれを支配の大義名分に利用し……　その一方、朝廷の政治介入は排したのだ」
"By taking the form of having the imperial court approve of its own administration, we used it for the cause of control while guaranteeing the authority of the imperial court ... On the other hand, we eliminated the political intervention of the imperial court."

「この良い所取りの手法は以後も延々と継承されている。　ごく短期の例外的な時代を除いて、現在に至るまで」
"This good way of taking things has been passed down endlessly to the present day, except in the very short-term exceptional times."

「六波羅でさえこの伝統は破れなかった。　権威と権力の二重構造は既に大和に根付いている。これを無理矢理に覆すより、利用した方が遥かに利益は大きいからだ……」
"Even Rokuhara did not break this tradition. The dual structure of authority and power is already rooted in Yamato, because it is far more profitable to use it than to overturn it ..."

教科書的な解説である。　だが勿論、歴史教師の真似事をするところに署長の目的があるわけではないだろう。
It is a textbook-like commentary. But, of course, the purpose of the chief is not to imitate a history teacher.

"For the administration that has already established control, the imperial court is nothing more than a portable shrine that has been used up. After that, it is enough if it is quietly stored in the warehouse so that it will not be used by others."

大将領足利護氏がいなくなれば、六波羅の支配体制には亀裂が入る。　四公方を中心とした派閥が表面化し、対立を始める事になろう。
Without General Ashikaga Moriuji, Rokuhara's rule would be cracked. Factions centered on the four officials will surface and start a conflict.

Taking the turmoil of the Rokuhara Shogunate as an opportunity, the expeditionary forces launch an attack-Shinnou assured that there was no such thing.

Shrines and temples are the heart of the local people. Therefore, in the olden days, defense equipment was sometimes set up so that it could work as a base to replace the castle due to military difficulties.

日光東照宮などはその最たる例であろう。　陽明門で名高いかの社は、徳川家が窮地に落ち江戸城退転となった場合に備える最終拠点でもあったのだと、一説に伝えられている。
Nikko Toshogu is a prime example. It is said that the company, which is famous for Yomei Gate, was also the final base in case the Tokugawa family fell into a predicament and retired from Edo Castle.

東照宮が徳川一門の守り神であったように、八幡宮は源氏の氏神。　古今東西の城砦に定番の地下構造を擁していても、驚くべきではないのかもしれない。
Just as Toshogu was the guardian deity of the Tokugawa clan, Hachimangu is the deity of Genji. It may not be surprising to have a classic underground structure in the eastern and western forts.

余りに都合が良すぎないか。

Bowing to the imperial court is one of the greatest sins for Yamato. I can't make a decision so easily ... But with Rokuhara, I can't say I won't do it.

"hostage?"

「奉刀参拝の当日、わしは普陀楽に置いとかれるんよ。　京都の朝廷が寄越してくる奉幣使の接待っちゅう名目で」
"On the day of worshiping the sword, I will be left in the comfort of the sword.

「……八幡宮別当であられる宮殿下と奉幣使が、祭礼に参加しないのですか？」
"... Isn't the palace and the messenger, who are the Betto of Hachimangu, participating in the festival?"

ある日、師は二人の弟子に刀を打たせた。　そして、彼らが刀を打ち上げると、それを川へ突き立てるよう命じた。
One day, the teacher had two disciples sword. And when they launched the sword, they ordered it to be thrust into the river.

まず、村正が刀を刺した。　そうして待っていると、やがて落葉が流れてきて、刃先に触れた。
First, Muramasa stabbed his sword. Then, as I waited, the fallen leaves flowed and touched the cutting edge.

あろうことか。　その刹那、ただ立っているだけの刀に当たった葉は、音もなく二つに切り裂かれて、下流へと漂っていった。
Is that what it is? At that moment, the leaf that hit the sword that was just standing was torn in two without sound and drifted downstream.

見守っていた弟子達は驚嘆し、村正は刀の恐るべき切れ味を誇って反り返った。　師は何も言わず、続いて正宗に試させた。
The disciples who were watching were amazed, and Muramasa turned back with the terrifying sharpness of the sword. The teacher didn't say anything and then let Masamune try it.

しばらく待つと、やがて同じように、川面を落葉が流れてきた。　人々は、正宗の刀も村正に匹敵する刃味を見せようかと、固唾を呑んで見守った。
After waiting for a while, the fallen leaves began to flow down the river surface in the same way. People watched with a sigh of breath, trying to show the blade of Masamune's sword comparable to that of Muramasa.

しかし、葉は刀に近付くと、まるで逃げるかの如く向きを変え、傷つかずに漂い去っていった。　それは幾度繰り返しても同じであった。正宗の刀は落葉を一枚たりと斬ることがなかった。
However, as the leaves approached the sword, they turned around as if they were running away and drifted away without being hurt. It was the same no matter how many times it was repeated. Masamune's sword never cut a single fallen leaf.

師は告げた。
The teacher told me.

――刃とは、斬るべきを自ずと斬り、斬らぬべきは自ずと斬らぬが最上である。　只の落葉を斬った村正は、葉を一枚も斬らなかった正宗の足元にも及ばぬと知るが良い――
――The best thing about a blade is to slash what you should slash, and not slash what you shouldn't slash. It is good to know that Muramasa, who cut the fallen leaves, does not even reach the feet of Masamune, who did not cut any leaves.

その言の通り。　正宗は天下一の名甲と尊ばれ、他方村正は呪われし妖甲と忌み嫌われ、後の世の評価に明暗を分けたのであった。
As the word says. Masamune was revered as the best in the world, while Muramasa was cursed and hated as a youkai, and divided the light and dark into the evaluation of the future world.

………… It is a myth.

村正と正宗が同一の師を戴いた事実はない。　両者の登場年代には隔たりがある。
There is no fact that Muramasa and Masamune had the same teacher. There is a gap between the two when they first appeared.

これは後世の数寄者が創作した物語に過ぎない。　　だが――村正と正宗、両者の真実の一端を伝えていないとは、おそらく言い得ぬであろう。
This is just a story created by a few posterity. But-it's hard to say that Muramasa and Masamune haven't told a part of the truth of both.

リフティングと呼ばれる基礎練習だろう。　球を地面に落とさぬよう蹴り続けるものだ……が、足利四郎のそれは世辞にも上手くなかった。

実際、邦氏の呑み込みの良さは意外な程だった。　三十分も経たない内に十回は確実に続けられるようになり、今は二十回の壁も越えて、更にその先を目指している。
In fact, the goodness of Kuniuji's swallowing was surprising. In less than thirty minutes, I was able to continue ten times without fail, and now I am aiming for the future beyond the barrier of twenty times.

才能があったのかもしれない。
Maybe he was talented.

「すごい……全然違う。　こうやれば良かったのか」
"Wow ... it's totally different. Should I have done this?"

"Thank you, break! Thanks to your teaching."

足利家の嫡子はリフティングに夢中になりながら、それでも声だけ俺へ寄越す。　少しならず驚いたせいで、返礼がやや遅れた。
The Ashikaga family's son is absorbed in lifting, but still only his voice moves to me. I was a little surprised, so the return was a little delayed.

……このような身分の少年が、こうも素直に下位の者へ礼を言うとは。
…… It is said that a boy with such status would thank the lower ranks obediently.

足利四郎邦氏は、どうやら良い気質を持って生まれたらしい。　彼を取り巻く環境が六波羅幕府というものであった事実を鑑みれば、奇跡的とさえ思える。
AshikagaShirouKuniuji seems to have been born with a good temperament. Considering the fact that the environment surrounding him was the Rokuhara Shogunate, it seems even miraculous.

(If this boy grows up like this ...)

The future of Yamato may not be so pessimistic. I also thought about that.

事実である。

It was selected because he was bought tall. When pushing a ball kicked in front of the goal, heading can be the decisive factor if you have an upper back.

できますと答えかけ、俺は慌てて口を閉ざした。　少年は追及して来なかった――ただ刹那、目の端に寂しさを過ぎらせたように見えた。
I answered that I could do it, and I closed my mouth in a hurry. The boy didn't pursue it-just momentarily, it seemed that he had passed loneliness at the edge of his eyes.

賢明な少年だ。　その賢明さが痛ましい。
A wise boy. That wiseness is painful.

Beside the boy, continue to give advice. I didn't care about the piercing gaze of the lady-in-waiters and the stunned guards.

逸れかけた球を少年の足先が捕まえ、引き戻す。　太腿で返し、もう一回。
The boy's toes catch the ball that is about to deviate and pull it back. Return with your thighs and try again.

山形の軌道で落ちてゆく。　地面にぶつかり、ぽん、ぽんと跳ね、転がり――
It falls in the orbit of Yamagata. Hit the ground, pop, pop, roll--

白い腕が、それを拾い上げた。

The men were here-to be exact, when they noticed Kuniuji's existence, they stabbed their knees on the spot. The first man remembers seeing it in the newspaper. Kyogoku Zenmon. He must be the secretary of the Shogunate Samurai-dokoro and the underwriter of the princess of Okabe.

六波羅は彼女の仇敵だ。　表に出さぬよう務めているからといって、恨み辛みがすぐさま消えて無くなるというものでもない。
Rokuhara is her enemy. Just because you try to keep it out of the open doesn't mean that the bitterness will disappear immediately.

足利四郎邦氏はその仇敵の頂点にある。　幕府に罪があるならば、その罪悪全ての責任保持者であるとも言い得る――岡部の乱当時はまだその座になかったものの。
AshikagaShirou Kuniuji is at the top of its enemy. If the shogunate is guilty, it can be said that it is responsible for all of its guilt-although it was not yet in that position at the time of the Okabe rebellion.

敵意以外の何かを抱くべき理由は、三千大千世界の果てまで探し求めたところで桜子姫には有るまい。　　だが――姫にも分かった筈だ。
There is no reason for Princess Sakurako to have something other than hostility when she searches to the ends of the 3,000-thousand-thousand world. But-the princess should have understood.

今彼女の前に立つ者は、ただ無心に遊んでいた少年に過ぎないのだと。　奇しくも、俺が彼をそうしてしまっていた。
The one who stands in front of her now is just a boy who was playing innocently. Strangely, I had done him that way.

眼差しに刃を秘めて見据えようと、打ち返してくる刃は無い。　無抵抗に貫通するだけなのだ……心まで。
There is no blade that hits back, trying to look at it with the blade hidden in the gaze. It just penetrates without resistance ... to the heart.

岡部の遺姫に、それができるのか。
Can Okabe's princess do that?

「……ふぅ」
"... Fu"

軽く両瞼を閉ざし、岡部桜子は一度吐息した。　何かを諦めたように見えた。
Gently closing both eyelids, Okabe Sakurako sighed once. It looked like I had given up something.

そうしてから京極善門に目で断りを入れ、邦氏の方へと歩み寄ってゆく。
After that, I turned down the Kyogoku Zenmon with my eyes and walked toward Kuniuji.

言葉を失う少年に、姫は微笑んだ。　表裏のない笑みだった。

Kuniuji gives an explanation that is completely insufficient to make an amateur understand. It wasn't a hassle, but simply because of a lack of vocabulary-perhaps sudden.

姫も困ったに違いない。　だが、顔の上では優しく目を細めるに留めた。

亡家の姫と。　覇者たるべき少年の。　　指先が――その一瞬、微かに触れ合ったようだった。
With the princess of the dead family. Of the boy who should be the champion. The fingertips-for that moment, seemed to touch each other.

桜子姫が一礼して帰ってゆく。　踵を返す挙措の中にさりげなく俺への会釈を混ぜて――
Princess Sakurako bows and goes home. In the process of returning the heel, casually mix a nod to me--

全く、何をやっているのだか。

少年は遠のく背を見詰めている。
The boy is staring at his back far away.

姫が男達の列に戻ると、彼らは立ち上がった。　再び歩き始める。
When the princess returned to the men's line, they stood up. Start walking again.

どうも本丸の一角――遊佐童心以下の閣老が詰める間の方角へと向かっているようだ。　姫に合わせてなのか、足取りは遅い。
It seems that the corner of the main enclosure is heading toward the direction where the elders under Yusa Doushin are squeezing. Perhaps it's for the princess, it's slow to walk.

Kuniuji doesn't seem to know her identity. It was clear that Princess Sakurako knew Kuniuji, so I was a little surprised.

しかし考えてみれば、当たり前か。　姫が足利四郎邦氏を見知る機会はいくらもあろうが、邦氏の方は、わざわざ敗軍の遺児を引見でもせぬ限り面識の持ちようがない。知らずとも不思議はなかった。
But when you think about it, is it natural? There are many opportunities for the princess to get to know Ashikaga Shirou Kuniuji, but Kuniuji has no acquaintance unless she takes the trouble to look at the orphans of the defeated army. No wonder I didn't know.

「あれなるは弾正尹従三位岡部頼綱が一女、桜子殿にございます」

The boy shook his body with a shocked look. --His Rokuhara, the daughter of a clan whose army of the shogunate has been destroyed.

彼女はこちらに斜め後姿を見せる格好で離れゆく。　沈着な様子ではあった。完璧ではなかったけれども。身ごなしの端々に覗く強張りは、姫の内心そのものに思えた。
She leaves with a slanted rear view. It looked like it was settled down. Though it wasn't perfect. The tension peeking into every corner of the body seemed to be the inner heart of the princess.

岡部頼綱の娘が、幕閣の面々の前へ連行されてゆくのだ。　心楽しい会合が待つ筈もなかった。
The daughter of Okabe Yoritsuna is taken to the front of the shogunate. I couldn't wait for a fun meeting.

おそらくは、岩田女史が俺に伝えた事――桜子奪取を謀る反幕勢力の存在について、査問を行うのだろう。　まさか拷問には掛けられまいが、度を超した尋問になる事は充分に有り得る。
Perhaps Ms. Iwata will inquire about what Ms. Iwata told me-the existence of anti-curtain forces plotting to seize Sakurako. It can be tortured, but it is quite possible that it will be an over-the-top cross-examination.

この普陀楽に、彼女の味方はいないのだから。　　去りゆく姫は美しかった。　荒野にただ一輪で咲く、孤独な花の美しさがあった。
There is no ally for her in this comfort. The leaving princess was beautiful. There was the beauty of a lonely flower that bloomed alone in the wilderness.

“…………”

少年は立ち尽くす。　指先を頬へ当てて。
The boy stands up. Place your fingertips on your cheeks.

It was a faint gesture to check the warmth that remained there.

心ここにあらぬ態となってしまった四郎邦氏の御前から退出し、城内の探査へ戻る。　南方面の曲輪を一巡りし、それから西へ。
Escape from the front of Shirou Kuniuji, who is in a state where his heart is not here, and return to exploration inside the castle. Go around the Kuruwa to the south and then head west.

西側の外郭には田畑や蔵、工場施設などが多い。　比較的重要度が低く、そのぶん長閑な区域だ。十歩進むたびに巡邏兵の疑り深い目と遭遇するような面倒はない。
There are many fields, warehouses, factory facilities, etc. in the outer hull on the west side. It is a relatively quiet area with relatively low importance. You don't have to worry about encountering the suspicious eyes of a patrol soldier every ten steps.

それはつまり、俺にとってあまり意味を持たないという事でもある。　早足に進み、より機密性の高い北部へ向かう。時間とは黄銅めいた黄金、浪費など許されない。
It also means that it doesn't make much sense to me. Go fast and head to the more confidential north. Time is brass gold, and no waste is allowed.

（奇縁か……宿縁か）
(Is it a strange relationship ... Is it an inn?)

回顧してそう想う。
I look back and think so.

足利邦氏と岡部桜子――勝者と敗者。滅ぼした者と滅ぼされた者。憎まれるべき者と憎むべき者。　一人の少年と一人の娘。
Ashikaga Kuniuji and Okabe Sakurako-Winners and losers. Those who have been destroyed and those who have been destroyed. Those who should be hated and those who should be hated. A boy and a daughter.

全く期せずして、その邂逅に立ち会ってしまった。　両者の住まう世界は俺には遠く、できる事など何もない。だが考えさせられずにはいられない。
Unexpectedly, I witnessed the encounter. The world they live in is far from me, and there is nothing I can do. But I can't help thinking.

どちらも背負うものが重過ぎる。年齢からすれば、苛酷なまでに。　二人の出会いはその難苦を少しでも和らげる結果に繋がるのだろうか。それともその逆となるか。
Both are too heavy to carry. To the point of age, it's harsh. Will the encounter between the two lead to a result that alleviates the hardship as much as possible? Or is it the other way around?

――前者であれば良い。　我が立場も忘れ、俺はふとそう願っていた。
--The former is fine. Forgetting my position, I suddenly wished so.

花畑を見下ろす峠道で、俺は足を止めた。
I stopped on the pass overlooking the flower garden.

女性が数人、賑々しく嬌声を上げながら花を摘んでいる。　農業に従事する下級労働者の作業という趣ではない。それなりに地位ある女官の戯れと見られた。
Several women are picking flowers with a lively roar. It is not the work of low-ranking workers engaged in agriculture. It was seen as a play of a lady-in-waiting with a certain position.

最初に注意を引かれたのはその光景のためである。　しかし注意を持続させねばならなかったのは、やや離れて彼女らを眺める孤影があったからだった。
The first thing that caught my attention was the sight. But I had to keep my attention because there was a lonely shadow looking at them at a distance.

他の誰でもない。　あれは、一条だ。
No one else. That is Ichijou.

少女は静かな視線をその凡庸な光景に注いでいる。　静けさは、無感動を意味するものとは違ったけれども――
The girl has a quiet gaze on the mediocre sight. Although tranquility was different from what meant apathy--

時間を云えば、まだ然程長くはない筈だが。　長さに見合わぬ多くの機会があった。綾弥一条なる人間を知る為の。
Speaking of time, it shouldn't be that long yet. There were many opportunities that were not worth the length. To know a human named Ayane Ichijou.

あれは、奇妙な娘だと思う。
I think it's a strange girl.

つくりものめいていると、そう感じる。　人形のよう、という印象とはまた違う。
I feel that way when I'm making things. It's different from the impression that it looks like a doll.

器械のようだと言い表すのが最も近い。
The closest thing to say is that it looks like an instrument.

人形じみた人間は、まず第一に虚ろである。　器の大きさに比してちっぽけな心しか感じられないから、ぽっかりと広い余剰空間が目に付くのだ。
Puppet-like humans are, first and foremost, hollow. Since I can only feel a small heart compared to the size of the vessel, I can see a large surplus space.

だから人間の抜け殻――人形だと見られる。　　一条は違う。　余剰空間が無い。
So it looks like a human shell-a doll. Ichijou is different. There is no surplus space.

正義の一念に固執するあの心は矮小にして狭小だ。　だが、それが相応に見えるのである。
That heart that sticks to justice is dwarf and narrow. But it looks reasonable.

少女の肉体は一つの意思、一つの理念、一つの目的を収める為だけのものなのだ。最初から。　それは人間ではない。　それは人形ではない。
The girl's body is only for one intention, one idea, and one purpose. From the beginning. It's not human. It's not a doll.

それは器械だ。
It's an instrument.

（あいつは、不幸なのだろうか）
(Is he unhappy?)

かつて胸に去来しなかったわけではないが、明確に言語化するのは今が初めてだった。　その一問。器械は不幸であるか。
It's not that I didn't come to my heart before, but it's the first time I've clearly verbalized it. That one question. Is the instrument unhappy?

人形は、きっと不幸であろう。　人の形に整えられながら人になれないのだから。
The doll will surely be unhappy. Because you can't become a person while being shaped into a person.

しかし器械はどうか。　器械として作られ器械として機能する器械。
But what about the instrument? An instrument that is made as an instrument and functions as an instrument.

それは不幸であるのか。　　俺には答えを出せなかった。
Is it unfortunate? I couldn't give an answer.

わかる事は一つきりだ。　それが不幸であろうと幸福であろうと、器械は己に与えられた単一機能を果たし続ける。
There is only one thing to understand. Whether it is unhappy or happy, the instrument continues to perform its single function.

壊れるまでずっと。
Until it breaks.

「あっ……湊斗さん」
"Ah ... Minato-san"

足音を聞いて振り返った一条が声を上げる。　呼んだのは実名の方だった。注意しておかねばならない――だが今はそんな気になれず、俺は黙って頷き返すに留めた。
Ichijou looks back after hearing the footsteps and raises his voice. It was the real name that I called. I have to be careful-but I don't feel like that now, so I just silently nodded.

どうせ誰も聞いてはいない。　花摘み娘の一団は自分達の会話に夢中だ。
No one is listening anyway. A group of flower-picking girls are crazy about their conversation.

「東側はもう一通り見たのか」
"Did you see another street on the east side?"

「いえ、まだ途中です」
"No, it's still on the way."

当たり前のように答える一条。　……ここは城の西部である。一条に割り当てた調査区域とは全く反対だ。が、俺はこれもいちいち指摘はせずにおいた。
Ichijou answers as a matter of course. ...... This is the western part of the castle. It's the exact opposite of the study area assigned to Ichijou. However, I didn't point out this one by one.

彼女を一人で行かせた時点で予測していた事だ。
That's what I expected when I sent her alone.

「湊斗さんの方はどうですか？」
"How about Minato-san?"

「それなりに収穫はあった。　詳しくは後で話そう」
"There was some harvest. I'll talk more about it later."

「はい」
"Okay"

快活な声だ。　しかし、間近で見ればさなきだに特異な少女の印象は更に明瞭だった。
A cheerful voice. However, when I saw it up close, the impression of the girl who was peculiar to Sanada was even clearer.

一条を良く観察する者が一人でもこの城にいれば、忽ちに正体は全て露見するのではないか。　……そう思いかけたのは流石に偏執的であったろうけれども。視線を戻して、花畑の娘を見る。
If there is even one person who observes Ichijou well in this castle, I think that all of his identity will be revealed. ...... I think it was paranoid, though. I look back and see the daughter in the flower garden.

無憂を唄って笑いさざめく彼女らとこの一条。距離はせいぜいが一〇メートル程だ。が――　精神の地平における隔たりは如何ばかりであろう。
These Ichijou with them singing melancholy and laughing. The distance is about 10 meters at most. But-what is the gap in the spiritual horizon?

傍らを見やれば、一条も俺の視線を追っていた。
Looking beside me, Ichijou was also following my gaze.

「……どう思いますか」
"……What do you think"

「あの女官達か」
"Are those lady-in-waiters?"

「この光景です」
"This is the scene"
